 "researchers began experimenting with the idea of research that was started a few years ago, in which it was believed that the rupture of a hair growing on the cranial skin could affect the environment around it and that reaction caused many at that location New hair can grow
 shodhakartaaon ne apane vichaar ke pareekshan ke liye ek chuuhe ke sharir ke 200 baalo ko alag alag vinyas main todaa

 isamen kaha gaya ki 1950 se 1982 ke dauraan chah raashtrapatiyon kaa kaarykaal rahaa or is dauraan keval ek kshamaa yachika ko khaarij kiya gaya jabaki 262 main mrityudand ko aaajeevan karawas main parivartit kar diya gaya
